S\u1ef1 \u00e1p l\u1ef1c n\u00e0y c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 t\u1ea1o ra c\u1ea3m gi\u00e1c c\u0103ng th\u1eb3ng v\u00e0 m\u1ec7t m\u1ecfi, \u0111\u1ed3ng th\u1eddi \u0111\u00f2i h\u1ecfi kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng th\u00edch \u1ee9ng v\u00e0 s\u00e1ng t\u1ea1o trong t\u00ecnh hu\u1ed1ng kh\u00f3 kh\u0103n.Tuy nhi\u00ean, n\u1ebfu bi\u1ebft c\u00e1ch qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd v\u00e0 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng \u00e1p l\u1ef1c m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch hi\u1ec7u qu\u1ea3, n\u00f3 c\u0169ng c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 l\u00e0 \u0111\u1ed9ng l\u1ef1c m\u1ea1nh m\u1ebd \u0111\u1ec3 ph\u00e1t tri\u1ec3n c\u00e1 nh\u00e2n v\u00e0 n\u00e2ng cao k\u1ef9 n\u0103ng l\u00e0m vi\u1ec7c.\n\ud83d\udc49V\u00e0 \u0111\u00e2y l\u00e0 nh\u1eefng tips c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 gi\u00fap b\u1ea1n gi\u1ea3m \u00e1p l\u1ef1c trong cv & cu\u1ed9c s\u1ed1ng \n1:X\u00e2y d\u1ef1ng k\u1ebf ho\u1ea1ch v\u00e0 \u01b0u ti\u00ean h\u00f3a c\u00f4ng vi\u1ec7c: T\u1ea1o ra m\u1ed9t l\u1ecbch tr\u00ecnh c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3, \u0111\u1eb7t \u01b0u ti\u00ean c\u00f4ng vi\u1ec7c quan tr\u1ecdng. \u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y gi\u00fap t\u1eadp trung v\u00e0o nhi\u1ec7m v\u1ee5 c\u1ea7n thi\u1ebft v\u00e0 tr\u00e1nh c\u1ea3m gi\u00e1c b\u1ecb \u00e1p \u0111\u1eb7t b\u1edfi qu\u00e1 nhi\u1ec1u c\u00f4ng vi\u1ec7c c\u00f9ng m\u1ed9t l\u00fac.\n2:H\u1ecdc c\u00e1ch n\u00f3i kh\u00f4ng: \u0110\u1eebng ng\u1ea7n ng\u1ea1i t\u1eeb ch\u1ed1i nh\u1eefng y\u00eau c\u1ea7u kh\u00f4ng th\u1ef1c s\u1ef1 quan tr\u1ecdng ho\u1eb7c kh\u00f4ng thu\u1ed9c tr\u00e1ch nhi\u1ec7m c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n. Bi\u1ebft c\u00e1ch gi\u1edbi h\u1ea1n v\u00e0 \u01b0u ti\u00ean nh\u1eefng vi\u1ec7c quan tr\u1ecdng h\u01a1n.\n3 :Th\u1ef1c h\u00e0nh self-care: Ch\u0103m s\u00f3c s\u1ee9c kho\u1ebb tinh th\u1ea7n v\u00e0 th\u1ec3 ch\u1ea5t l\u00e0 quan tr\u1ecdng. \u0102n \u0111\u00fang c\u00e1ch, t\u1eadp th\u1ec3 d\u1ee5c, ng\u1ee7 \u0111\u1ee7 gi\u1ea5c, v\u00e0 th\u1ef1c h\u00e0nh c\u00e1c k\u1ef9 thu\u1eadt gi\u1ea3m c\u0103ng th\u1eb3ng nh\u01b0 h\u01a1i th\u1edf s\u00e2u, yoga, ho\u1eb7c thi\u1ec1n.\n4:H\u1ecdc c\u00e1ch qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd th\u1eddi gian: S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng c\u00e1c k\u1ef9 thu\u1eadt qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd th\u1eddi gian nh\u01b0 ph\u00e2n t\u00edch Pareto (nguy\u00ean t\u1eafc 80/20), k\u1ef9 thu\u1eadt Pomodoro (c\u00f4ng ngh\u1ec7 h\u1eb9n gi\u1edd), ho\u1eb7c \u00e1p d\u1ee5ng nguy\u00ean t\u1eafc Eisenhower (ph\u00e2n lo\u1ea1i nhi\u1ec7m v\u1ee5 theo m\u1ee9c \u0111\u1ed9 quan tr\u1ecdng v\u00e0 kh\u1ea9n c\u1ea5p).\n5:T\u1eadp trung v\u00e0o vi\u1ec7c m\u1ed9t nhi\u1ec7m v\u1ee5 m\u1ed9t l\u00fac: \u0110\u1eebng c\u1ed1 g\u1eafng l\u00e0m nhi\u1ec1u c\u00f4ng vi\u1ec7c c\u00f9ng m\u1ed9t l\u00fac, \u0111i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 d\u1eabn \u0111\u1ebfn s\u1ef1 ph\u00e2n t\u00e2m v\u00e0 m\u1ea5t th\u1eddi gian. Hai b\u00e0 c\u00f9ng Thi S\u00e1ch chi\u00eau m\u1ed9 ngh\u0129a qu\u00e2n, chu\u1ea9n b\u1ecb kh\u1edfi ngh\u0129a, nh\u01b0ng Thi S\u00e1ch b\u1ecb T\u00f4 \u0110\u1ecbnh gi\u1ebft ch\u1ebft. H\u1eadn gi\u1eb7c h\u00e3m h\u1ea1i nh\u00e2n d\u00e2n, gi\u1ebft h\u1ea1i ch\u1ed3ng m\u00ecnh, Tr\u01b0ng Tr\u1eafc \u0111\u00e3 c\u00f9ng em g\u00e1i Tr\u01b0ng Nh\u1ecb ph\u00e1t \u0111\u1ed9ng cu\u1ed9c kh\u1edfi ngh\u0129a \u1edf c\u1eeda S\u00f4ng H\u00e1t tr\u00ean S\u00f4ng H\u1ed3ng (thu\u1ed9c \u0111\u1ecba ph\u1eadn huy\u1ec7n Ph\u00fac Th\u1ecd, t\u1ec9nh H\u00e0 T\u00e2y).\n\u2744\ufe0fCu\u1ed9c kh\u1edfi ngh\u0129a c\u1ee7a Hai B\u00e0 Tr\u01b0ng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c nh\u00e2n d\u00e2n kh\u1eafp n\u01a1i \u1ee7ng h\u1ed9, t\u1ea1o th\u00e0nh s\u1ee9c m\u1ea1nh nh\u01b0 v\u0169 b\u00e3o, \u0111\u00e1nh \u0111u\u1ed5i T\u00f4 \u0110\u1ecbnh ph\u1ea3i b\u1ecf ch\u1ea1y v\u1ec1 n\u01b0\u1edbc. D\u01b0\u1edbi s\u1ef1 l\u00e3nh \u0111\u1ea1o c\u1ee7a Hai B\u00e0 Tr\u01b0ng, nhi\u1ec1u cu\u1ed9c kh\u1edfi ngh\u0129a \u0111\u1ecba ph\u01b0\u01a1ng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c th\u1ed1ng nh\u1ea5t th\u00e0nh m\u1ed9t phong tr\u00e0o r\u1ed9ng l\u1edbn t\u1eeb mi\u1ec1n xu\u00f4i \u0111\u1ebfn mi\u1ec1n n\u00fai, bao g\u1ed3m c\u1ea3 ng\u01b0\u1eddi Vi\u1ec7t v\u00e0 c\u00e1c d\u00e2n t\u1ed9c kh\u00e1c trong n\u01b0\u1edbc \u00c2u L\u1ea1c c\u0169.\n\u2744\ufe0fCh\u1ec9 trong m\u1ed9t th\u1eddi gian ng\u1eafn, Hai B\u00e0 Tr\u01b0ng \u0111\u00e3 \u0111\u00e1nh chi\u1ebfm \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c 65 huy\u1ec7n th\u00e0nh, ngh\u0129a l\u00e0 to\u00e0n b\u1ed9 l\u00e3nh th\u1ed5 n\u01b0\u1edbc Vi\u1ec7t h\u1ed3i \u0111\u00f3. It exists in digital form and is issued by the Central Bank. In this article, let's learn more about what CBDC is!\n\nWhat is CBDC?\n\nCBDC (Central Bank Digital Currency) or Central Bank Electronic Currency is a digital currency issued and managed by the Central Bank of a country.\n\nThe purpose of this currency is to replace or supplement cash and deposits in the country's financial system.\n\nCBDCs can be used like conventional currencies to pay for products and services. It can be stored in e-wallets or online bank accounts.\n\nCountries are researching and implementing CBDC as part of efforts to modernize their financial systems, reduce dependence on cash, and increase the efficiency and safety of financial transactions.\n\nWhat are the benefits of CBDC?\n\nHere are some notable benefits of CBDC:\n\nIncrease the safety of the financial system\n\nCompared to cash or traditional payment methods, CBDC is money in electronic form so it is more difficult to counterfeit. However, to ensure safety against cyber attacks or fraud, the infrastructure of the CBDC system also needs to be well protected.\n\nStrengthening the supervision capacity of the Central Bank (Central Bank)\n\nCBDC allows the Central Bank to monitor financial transactions more closely, ensuring compliance with the country's financial policies and regulations. Each CBDC coin, depending on the technology chosen, can be traced back to every transaction related to it since its issuance.\n\nThis is also different from cryptocurrencies that operate anonymously on other blockchains such as Ethereum, Bitcoin...\n\nEnhance convenience and flexibility\n\nCBDC can be used and converted across digital platforms quickly and easily. In times of crisis, having the ability to quickly convert between CBDC and traditional currencies can help optimize payment and transaction management.\n\nMinimize the impact of the crisis\n\nCBDC uses blockchain technology or other distributed technology, helping to increase transparency in financial transactions. This can help prevent fraud, money laundering and illegal financial activity, thereby reducing financial risk and creating a safer financial environment during times of crisis.\n\nCost savings\n\nCBDC can reduce costs associated with the production, distribution and management of cash, enhancing the efficiency of financial transactions. In fact, transporting and preserving cash will incur many costs. With large transactions, tallying a large amount of money costs time, effort and can cause errors in counting. In contrast, CBDC will not have these problems.\n\nWhat are the risks of CBDC?\n\nBesides the above notable benefits, CBDC also has many potential risks as follows:\n\nPrivacy and security risks\n\nCBDC is considered safer and more convenient than cash or traditional payment methods. However, it may increase the risk of personal information disclosure. It can also become a target of cyber attacks and online fraud.\n\nImpact on financial markets\n\nCBDC can lead to the movement of account balances from Commercial Banks to accounts opened at Central Banks. This could weaken the traditional role of Commercial Banks and change the overall structure of the financial system.\n\nDependence on technology\n\nCBDC depends on blockchain technology or other digital financial technologies. Therefore, it may face problems related to ensuring stable operation and adaptability to changes for both users and adopting organizations.\n\nLegal and regulatory issues\n\nImplementing a CBDC requires new legal regulations and policies to ensure its safety, security, and controllability. At the same time, it must ensure fairness to all individuals and organizations\n\n#cbdc #DigitalCurrency #entryprenuer #financialfreedom #makemoneyonline #BYBIT #BTC", "replyCount": 22, c\u1ee7a nh\u00e0 n\u01b0\u1edbc, c\u00f2n m\u1ea1ng s\u1ed1ng l\u00e0 c\u1ee7a c\u00e1c ng\u01b0\u1eddi\u201d. T\u1ea5t c\u1ea3 m\u1ecdi ng\u01b0\u1eddi c\u00f3 m\u1eb7t trong ng\u00e2n h\u00e0ng \u0111\u1ec1u c\u00fai \u0111\u1ea7u im l\u1eb7ng n\u1eb1m xu\u1ed1ng.\n\n\u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c g\u1ecdi l\u00e0: \u201cC\u00e1ch th\u1ee9c khai t\u00e2m \u2013 Thay \u0111\u1ed5i nh\u1eefng suy ngh\u0129 theo l\u1ed1i m\u00f2n\u201d.\n\n\u2013 M\u1ed9t c\u00f4 g\u00e1i n\u1eb1m tr\u00ean b\u00e0n trong t\u01b0 th\u1ebf k\u00edch th\u00edch khi\u00eau g\u1ee3i, t\u00ean c\u01b0\u1edbp c\u1ea7m \u0111\u1ea7u la to: \u201cXin h\u00e3y c\u01b0 x\u1eed v\u0103n minh, ch\u00fang t\u00f4i l\u00e0 c\u01b0\u1edbp ch\u1ee9 kh\u00f4ng ph\u1ea3i nh\u1eefng k\u1ebb hi\u1ebfp d\u00e2m b\u1ec7nh ho\u1ea1n!\u201d\n\n\u0110\u00e2y \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c g\u1ecdi l\u00e0 \u201cL\u00e0m vi\u1ec7c chuy\u00ean nghi\u1ec7p \u2013 Ch\u1ec9 t\u1eadp trung v\u00e0o c\u00f4ng vi\u1ec7c m\u00e0 b\u1ea1n \u0111ang l\u00e0m!\u201d\n\n\u2013 Khi t\u00ean c\u01b0\u1edbp quay l\u1ea1i, m\u1ed9t t\u00ean c\u01b0\u1edbp tr\u1ebb h\u01a1n (c\u00f3 b\u1eb1ng MBA) n\u00f3i v\u1edbi t\u00ean c\u01b0\u1edbp gi\u00e0 h\u01a1n (k\u1ebb m\u1edbi t\u1ed1t nghi\u1ec7p h\u1ebft ph\u1ed5 th\u00f4ng): \u201c\u0110\u1ea1i ca, ch\u00fang ta c\u00f3 c\u1ea7n \u0111\u1ebfm s\u1ed1 ti\u1ec1n c\u01b0\u1edbp \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u00e0 bao nhi\u00eau kh\u00f4ng?\u201d. T\u00ean c\u01b0\u1edbp gi\u00e0 g\u1eb1n gi\u1ecdng: \u201cM\u00e0y ngu l\u1eafm, nhi\u1ec1u ti\u1ec1n th\u1ebf, l\u00e0m sao m\u00e0 \u0111\u1ebfm \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c? \u0110\u1ee3i \u0111i, t\u1ed1i nay tr\u00ean tivi s\u1ebd n\u00f3i ch\u00fang ta c\u01b0\u1edbp \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c bao nhi\u00eau ti\u1ec1n!\u201d\n\n\u0110\u00e2y \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c g\u1ecdi l\u00e0: \u201cKinh nghi\u1ec7m \u2013 Ng\u00e0y nay th\u00ec kinh nghi\u1ec7m quan tr\u1ecdng h\u01a1n b\u1eb1ng c\u1ea5p, s\u00e1ch v\u1edf\u201d\n\n\u2013 Sau khi nh\u1eefng t\u00ean c\u01b0\u1edbp t\u1ea9u tho\u00e1t, gi\u00e1m \u0111\u1ed1c ng\u00e2n h\u00e0ng \u0111ang \u0111\u1ecbnh g\u1ecdi b\u00e1o c\u1ea3nh s\u00e1t.
